     Ok(count as u64)\n509\t    }\n510\t\n511\t    async fn job_enqueue(&self, job: &Job) -> Result<()> {\n512\t        self.execute(\n513\t            \"INSERT INTO jobs (id, type, params, state, &job.job_type,\n518\t                &job.params,\n519\t                &job.state.to_string(),\n520\t                &job.claimed_by.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"\"),\n521\t                &job.claim_expires_at.map(|v| v as i64).unwrap_or(0),\n522\t                &job.progress,\n523\t            ] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n524\t        )?;\n525\t        Ok(())\n526\t    }\n527\t\n528\t    async fn job_dequeue(&self, worker_id: &str) -> Result<Option<Job>> {\n529\t        // Start a transaction\n530\t        let conn = self\n531\t            .conn\n532\t            .lock()\n533\t            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n534\t        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n535\t\n536\t        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n537\t        let expires_at = now + (5 * 60 * 1000); // 5 minutes from now\n538\t\n539\t        // Find and claim a job\n540\t        let job_id: Option<String> = tx\n541\t            .query_row(\n542\t                \"SELECT id FROM jobs WHERE state = 'queued' ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 1\",\n543\t                [],\n544\t                |row| row.get(0),\n545\t            )\n546\t            .ok();\n547\t\n548\t        if let Some(ref job_id) = job_id {\n549\t            tx.execute(\n550\t                \"UPDATE jobs SET state = 'in_progress', claimed_by = ?1, claim_expires_at = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n551\t                [\n552\t                    &worker_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n553\t                    &expires_at as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n554\t                    job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n555\t                ],\n556\t            )?;\n557\t\n558\t            // Fetch the updated job\n559\t            let job: Job = tx.query_row(\n560\t                \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress\n561\t                 FROM jobs WHERE id = ?1\",\n562\t                [job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n563\t                |row| {\n564\t                    Ok(Job {\n565\t                        id: row.get(0)?,\n566\t                        job_type: row.get(1)?,\n567\t                        params: row.get(2)?,\n568\t                        state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n569\t                        claimed_by: {\n570\t                            let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n571\t                            if claimed.is_empty() {\n572\t                                None\n573\t                            } else {\n574\t                                Some(claimed)\n575\t                            }\n576\t                        },\n577\t                        claim_expires_at: {\n578\t                            let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n579\t                            if expires == 0 {\n580\t                                None\n581\t                            } else {\n582\t                                Some(expires as u64)\n583\t                            }\n584\t                        },\n585\t                        progress: row.get(6)?,\n586\t                    })\n587\t                },\n588\t            )?;\n589\t\n590\t            tx.commit()?;\n591\t            Ok(Some(job))\n592\t        } else {\n593\t            tx.commit()?;\n594\t            Ok(None)\n595\t        }\n596\t    }\n597\t\n598\t    async fn job_update_status(\n599\t        &self,\n600\t        job_id: &str,\n601\t        status: JobState,\n602\t        result: Option<&str>,\n603\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n604\t        self.execute(\n605\t            \"UPDATE jobs SET state = ?1, progress = ?2 WHERE id = ?3\",\n606\t            &[\n607\t                &status.to_string(),\n608\t  }\n650\t\n651\t    async fn job_list(&self, status: Option<JobState>, limit: usize) -> Result<Vec<Job>> {\n652\t        let mut sql =\n653\t            \"SELECT id, type, params, state, claimed_by, claim_expires_at, progress FROM jobs\"\n654\t                .to_string();\n655\t\n656\t        if status.is_some() {\n657\t            sql.push_str(\" WHERE state = ?\");\n658\t        }\n659\t\n660\t        sql.push_str(&format!(\" ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT {limit}\"));\n661\t\n662\t        let status_str: Option<String> = status.map(|s| s.to_string());\n663\t        let params: {\n669\t            Ok(Job {\n670\t                id: row.get(0)?,\n671\t                job_type: row.get(1)?,\n672\t                params: row.get(2)?,\n673\t                state: row.get::<_,    Some(expires as u64)\n688\t                    }\n689\t                },\n690\t                progress: row.get(6)?,\n691\t            })\n692\t        })\n693\t    }\n694\t\n695\t    async fn leader_lease_acquire(&self, lease: &LeaderLease) -> Result<bool> {\n696\t        let conn = self\n697\t            .conn\n698\t            .lock()\n699\t            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n700\t        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n701\t\n702\t        // Check if there's an existing valid lease\n703\t        let existing: Option<(String, u64)> = tx\n704\t            .query_row(\n705\t                \"SELECT scope, expires_at FROM leader_lease WHERE expires_at > ?1\",\n706\t                [&(chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64) as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n707\t                |row| Ok((row.get(0)?, row.get(1)?)),\n708\t            )\n709\t            .ok();\n710\t\n711\t        let acquired = if existing.is_some() {\n712\t            false\n713\t        } else {\n714\t            tx.execute(\n715\t                \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO leader_lease (scope, holder, expires_at)\n716\t                 VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)\",\n717\t                [\n718\t                    &lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n719\t                    &lease.holder,\n720\t                    &lease.expires_at,\n721\t                ],\n722\t            )?;\n723\t            true\n724\t        };\n725\t\n726\t        tx.commit()?;\n727\t        Ok(acquired)\n728\t jobs\"\n                .to_string();\n\n        if status.is_some() {\n            sql.push_str(\" WHERE state = ?\");\n        }\n\n        sql.push_str(&format!(\" ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT {limit}\"));\n\n        let status_str: Option<String> = status.map(|s| s.to_string());\n        let params: Vec<&dyn rusqlite::ToSql> = match &status_str {\n            Some(s) => vec![s],\n            None => vec![],\n        };\n\n        self.query_map(&sql, &params, |row| {\n            Ok(Job {\n                id: row.get(0)?,\n                job_type: row.get(1)?,\n                params: row.get(2)?,\n                state: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n                claimed_by: {\n                    let claimed: String = row.get(4)?;\n                    if claimed.is_empty() {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(claimed)\n                    }\n                },\n                claim_expires_at: {\n                    let expires: i64 = row.get(5)?;\n                    if expires == 0 {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(expires as u64)\n                    }\n                },\n                progress: row.get(6)?,\n            })\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_acquire(&self, lease: &LeaderLease) -> Result<bool> {\n        let conn = self\n            .conn\n            .lock()\n            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n\n        // Check if there's an existing valid lease\n        let existing: Option<(String, u64)> = tx\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT scope, expires_at FROM leader_lease WHERE expires_at > ?1\",\n                [&(chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64) as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| Ok((row.get(0)?, row.get(1)?)),\n            )\n            .ok();\n\n        let acquired = if existing.is_some() {\n            false\n        } else {\n            tx.execute(\n                \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO leader_lease (scope, holder, expires_at)\n                 VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)\",\n                [\n                    &lease.scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                    &lease.holder,\n                    &lease.expires_at,\n                ],\n            )?;\n            true\n        };\n\n        tx.commit()?;\n        Ok(acquired)\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_release(&self, scope: &str) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"DELETE FROM leader_lease WHERE scope = ?1\",\n            &[&scope as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_get(&self) -> Result<Option<LeaderLease>> {\n        let result: Option<LeaderLease> = self\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT scope, holder, expires_at FROM leader_lease LIMIT 1\",\n                &[] as &[&dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| {\n                    Ok(LeaderLease {\n                        scope: row.get(0)?,\n                        holder: row.get(1)?,\n                        expires_at: row.get(2)?,\n                    })\n                },\n            )\n            .ok();\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    async fn canary_upsert(&self, canary: &Canary) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO canaries (id, name, index_uid, interval_s, self\n            .conn\n            .lock()\n            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        // Execute a simple query to check if the database is responsive\n        let init_schema(conn: &Connection) -> Result<()> {\n        // Table 1: Tasks\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tasks (\n                miroir_id   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                created_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                status      TEXT NOT NULL,\n                node_tasks  TEXT NOT NULL,\n                error       TEXT\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 2: Node settings version\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS node_settings_version (\n                index_uid   TEXT NOT NULL,\n                node_id     TEXT NOT NULL,\n                version     INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at  INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                PRIMARY KEY (index_uid, node_id)\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 3: Aliases\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aliases (\n                name          TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                kind          TEXT NOT NULL,\n                current_uid   TEXT,\n                target_uids   TEXT,\n                version       INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at    INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                history       TEXT NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 4: Sessions\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (\n                session_id            TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                last_write_mtask_id   TEXT,\n                last_write_at         INTEGER,\n                pinned_group          INTEGER,\n                min_settings_version  INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                ttl                   INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 5: Idempotency cache\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS idempotency_cache (\n                key              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                body_sha256      BLOB NOT NULL,\n                miroir_task_id   TEXT NOT NULL,\n                expires_at       INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 6: Jobs\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS jobs (\n                id                 TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                type               TEXT NOT NULL,\n                params             TEXT NOT NULL,\n                state              TEXT NOT NULL,\n                claimed_by         TEXT,\n                claim_expires_at   INTEGER,\n                progress           TEXT NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 7: Leader lease\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS leader_lease (\n                scope        TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                holder       TEXT NOT NULL,\n                expires_at   INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 8: Canaries\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS canaries (\n                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                name TEXT NOT NULL,\n                index_uid TEXT NOT NULL,\n                interval_s INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                query_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                assertions_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                enabled INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 9: Canary runs\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS canary_runs (\n                canary_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n                ran_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                status TEXT NOT NULL,\n                latency_ms INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                failed_assertions_json TEXT,\n                PRIMARY KEY (canary_id, ran_at)\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 10: CDC cursors\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cdc_cursors (\n                sink_name TEXT NOT NULL,\n                index_uid TEXT NOT NULL,\n                last_event_seq INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                PRIMARY KEY (sink_name, index_uid)\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 11: Tenant map\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tenant_map (\n                api_key_hash BLOB PRIMARY KEY,\n                tenant_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n                group_id INTEGER\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 12: Rollover policies\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS rollover_policies (\n                name TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                write_alias TEXT NOT NULL,\n                read_alias TEXT NOT NULL,\n                pattern TEXT NOT NULL,\n                triggers_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                retention_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                template_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                enabled INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 13: Search UI config\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS search_ui_config (\n                index_uid TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                config_json TEXT NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 14: Admin sessions\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS admin_sessions (\n                session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                csrf_token TEXT NOT NULL,\n                admin_key_hash TEXT NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                expires_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                revoked INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n
